The defendant agrees and stipulates that the factual allegations set forth in the Statement of Facts, attached hereto and incorporated herein as Exhibit 2, are true and correct and accurately reflect the defendant&#8217;s criminal conduct.  The parties further stipulate and agree to the Statement of Facts attached hereto and incorporated herein as Exhibit 2.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:center;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;font-weight:bold;">Defendant&#8217;s Waiver of Rights, Including the Right to Trial and Appeal</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;padding-left:8px;text-indent:48px;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">The defendant represents to the Court that defendant is satisfied that the defendant&#8217;s attorneys have rendered effective assistance.  Defendant understands that by entering into this Agreement, the defendant surrenders certain rights as provided in this Agreement.  Defendant understands that the rights of defendants include the following:</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:center;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">4</font></div><br><hr style="page-break-after:always"><a name="s9BCE986408BC263D8D36533CC33AB8A8"></a><div></div><br><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-left:8px;padding-top:4px;text-align:left;text-indent:96px;"><font style="padding-top:4px;text-align:left;font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;color:#010000;padding-right:48px;">a.</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">If the defendant persisted in a plea of not guilty to the charges, defendant would have the right to a speedy jury trial with the assistance of counsel. The trial may be conducted by a judge sitting without a jury if the defendant, the United States, and the Court all agree.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-top:1px;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-left:8px;text-align:left;text-indent:96px;"><font style="text-align:left;font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;color:#010000;padding-right:48px;">b.</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">At a trial, the United States would be required to present its witnesses and other evidence against the defendant.  The defendant would be able to confront those witnesses and the defendant&#8217;s attorney would be able to cross-examine them. In turn, the defendant could, but would not be required to, present witnesses and other evidence on its own behalf. If the witnesses for the defendant would not appear voluntarily, the defendant could require their attendance through the subpoena power of the Court.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-top:1px;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-left:8px;text-align:left;text-indent:96px;"><font style="text-align:left;font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;color:#010000;padding-right:48px;">c.</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">At a trial, no inference of guilt could be drawn from the defendant&#8217;s refusal to present evidence.  However, if the defendant desired to do so, it could present evidence on its behalf.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;padding-left:8px;text-indent:48px;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">The defendant understands that nothing in this Agreement will restrict access by the United States Probation Office or the Court to information and records in the possession of the United States or any of its investigative law enforcement agencies, including state and local law enforcement agencies, as well as information, documents and records obtained from the defendant.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;padding-left:8px;text-indent:48px;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">The defendant is aware that Title 18, United States Code, Section 3742 affords a defendant the right to appeal the sentence imposed. Should the Court impose the sentence proposed herein, the defendant agrees that it will waive the right to appeal the plea, conviction, and sentence (or the manner in which it was determined) on the grounds set forth in Title 18, United States Code, Section 3742.  This Agreement does not affect the rights or obligations of the United States as set forth in Title 18, United States Code, Section 3742(b).</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;padding-left:8px;text-indent:48px;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">The defendant is also aware that the United States Constitution and the laws of the United States afford the defendant the right to contest or &#8220;collaterally attack&#8221; its conviction or sentence after the conviction has become final. Knowing that, the defendant knowingly waives the right to contest or &#8220;collaterally attack&#8221; the defendant&#8217;s plea, conviction, and sentence, provided that such sentence is consistent with the terms of this Agreement, by means of any post-conviction proceeding.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;padding-left:8px;text-indent:48px;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">The defendant waives all defenses based on the statute of limitations with respect to any prosecution relating to the conduct described in the attached Statement of Facts that is not time- barred on the date that this Agreement is signed in the event that: (a) the conviction is later vacated for any reason; (b) the defendant violates this Agreement; or (c) the plea is later withdrawn, provided that such prosecution is brought within one year of any such vacation of conviction, violation of the agreement, or withdrawal of the plea plus the remaining time period of the statute of limitations as of the date that this Agreement is signed. The Department is free to take any position on appeal or any other post-judgment matter.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="page-break-after:always"><a name="sAC2392DBB11B035EB47E533CC369C566"></a><div></div><br><div conduct charged in the Information based on venue, speedy trial under the United States Constitution and Speedy Trial Act, and any and all constitutional and non-jurisdictional style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div for a violation of Title 18, United States Code, Section 371, is a fine of $500,000 or twice the gross gain or gross loss resulting from the offense, whichever is greatest, 18 U.S.C. &#167; 3571(c)(3), (d); five years&#8217; probation, 18 U.S.C. &#167; 3561(c)(1); and a mandatory special assessment of $400, 18 U.S.C. &#167; 3013(a)(2)(B).</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">The defendant hereby stipulates and agrees not to institute or participate in any proceeding to interfere with, alter, or bar enforcement of any fine, penalty, special assessment, or forfeiture order pursuant to the automatic stay or other provision of the United States Bankruptcy Code.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div The Court will then determine a reasonable sentence within the statutory range after considering the advisory sentencing guideline range and the factors listed in 18 U.S.C. &#167; 3553(a). appropriate in this case, as the defendant&#8217;s parent corporation, Avon Products,</font></div><br><hr style="page-break-after:always"><a time of sentencing the mandatory special assessment of $400 per count.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font Bound.</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">This agreement is presented to the Court pursuant to Fed. R. Crim. P. 11(c)(1)(C). The defendant understands that, if the Court rejects this Agreement, the Court must: (a) inform the parties that the Court rejects the Agreement; (b) advise the defendant&#8217;s counsel that the Court is not required to follow the Agreement and afford the defendant the opportunity to withdraw its plea; and (c) advise the defendant that if the plea is not withdrawn, the Court may dispose of the case less favorably toward the defendant than the Agreement contemplated. The defendant further understands that if the Court refuses to accept any provision of this Agreement, neither party shall be bound by the provisions of the Agreement.  The defendant, however, also understands that if the Court accepts this Agreement, the Court is bound by the sentencing recommendations in paragraph 22.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:center;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;font-weight:bold;">Consolidation of Plea and Sentencing and Waiver of Presentence Investigation</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;padding-left:8px;text-indent:48px;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">The parties agree, subject to the Court&#8217;s approval, to waive the requirement for a presentence report, pursuant to Federal Rule of Criminal Procedure 32(c)(1)(A), based on a finding by the Court that the record contains information sufficient to enable the Court to meaningfully exercise its sentencing power.  The parties, however, agree that in the event the Court orders the preparation of a presentence report prior to sentencing, such order will not affect the agreement set forth herein.  Additionally, if the Court directs the preparation of a presentence report, the Department will fully inform the preparer of the presentence report and the Court of the facts and law related to the defendant&#8217;s case.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;padding-left:8px;text-indent:48px;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">The parties further agree to request that the Court combine the entry of the guilty plea and sentencing into one proceeding. The parties, however, agree that in the event the Court orders that the entry of the guilty plea and sentencing hearing occur at separate proceedings, such an order will not affect the Agreement set forth herein.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:center;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;font-weight:bold;">Breach of the Plea Agreement</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;padding-left:8px;text-indent:48px;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">If the defendant breaches the terms of this Agreement, or commits any new criminal offense between signing this Agreement and sentencing, the Department is relieved of its obligations under this Agreement, but the defendant may not withdraw its guilty plea. Whether the defendant has breached any provision of this Agreement shall be determined solely by the Department.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;padding-left:8px;text-indent:48px;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">In the event the Department determines that the defendant has breached this Agreement, the Department agrees to provide the defendant with written notice of such breach prior to</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:center;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">8</font></div><br><hr style="page-break-after:always"><a name="sBC11DFC382BE8D5C16FB533CC3F5D6A6"></a><div></div><br><div style="line-height:120%;padding-top:4px;text-align:left;padding-left:8px;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">instituting any prosecution resulting from such breach. Within thirty (30) days of receipt of such notice, the defendant shall have the opportunity to respond to the Department in writing to explain the nature and circumstances of such breach, as well as the actions the defendant has taken to address and remediate the situation, which explanation the Department shall consider in determining whether to pursue prosecution of the defendant.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;padding-left:56px;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">In the event of a breach of this Agreement by the defendant:</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-left:8px;text-align:left;text-indent:96px;"><font style="text-align:left;font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;color:#010000;padding-right:48px;">a.</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">AVON CHINA shall be fully subject to criminal prosecution for any crimes, including perjury and obstruction of justice;</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-top:1px;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-left:8px;text-align:left;text-indent:96px;"><font style="text-align:left;font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;color:#010000;padding-right:48px;">b.</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">the Department will be free to use against AVON CHINA, directly and indirectly, in any criminal or civil proceeding any of the information or materials provided by AVON CHINA pursuant to this Agreement, as well as the admitted Statement of Facts contained herein; and</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-top:1px;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-left:8px;text-align:left;text-indent:96px;"><font style="text-align:left;font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;color:#010000;padding-right:48px;">c.</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">should the Department elect to pursue criminal charges or any civil action that was not filed as a result of this Agreement, then AVON CHINA agrees that any applicable statute of limitations is tolled between the date of AVON CHINA&#8217;S signing of this Agreement and the discovery by the Department of any breach by AVON CHINA, and AVON CHINA waives all defenses based on the statute of limitations, venue, any claim of pre-indictment delay, or any speedy trial claim with respect to any such prosecution or action, except to the extent that such defenses existed as of the date of the signing of this Agreement.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:center;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;font-weight:bold;">Complete Agreement</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;padding-left:8px;text-indent:48px;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">This written Agreement constitutes the complete plea agreement between the parties. No promises or representations have been made by the United States except as set forth in writing in this Agreement.  The defendant acknowledges that no threats have been made against the defendant and that the defendant is pleading guilty freely and voluntarily because the defendant is guilty. Any modification of this Agreement shall be valid only as set forth in writing in a supplemental or revised plea agreement signed by all parties.</font></div><div
